 isamen centre ke kathor bhoomi adhigrahan vidheyak 2013 ke praavdhaanon ko kamatar kiya gaya he
 The bill removes social impact assessment and consent rules for acquiring land for public purposes, industrial corridors and public-private partnership schemes

 "he said," We will implement the new law in the state from 15 August on Independence Day
 '' rajya sarkaar ise 15 agast se pehle kanoon ke rup main adhishuchet kar degi

 While doing some research on Subhash Chandra Bose, one of the greatest architects of India's independence, i have known that the Ford Motor Company gave its new V-8 car for free to the use of Congress ministers during the Haripura session of 1938
 Since then, this honor has completely changed into amazement
 america auto company ke sansthaapak henry ford apni essembly line ke liye prasiddh the; lekin sadbhaavna ke nivesh ke rup main yah unki pratibha kii pahchaan thi
 With this initiative, he ensured the convenience of India much earlier
 yah ansh subhash chandra bose kii mihir bose dwaara likhit jeevani se he
 During a search for confirmation of Ford's imaginative seduction at Leonard Gordon's Brothers Against the Raj on Subhash Chandra Bose, i came to know that Bose was actually taken to a congressional camp town on a chariot donated by a local respected person Gaya was engaged in '51 strong bulls
 un dinon congress kaa vishisht vaahan kisaanon kii baiylgaadee hi thi, ise 1952 ke baad congress kaa chunaav chinh bhi banaaya janaa tha
 But this symbolism, including the strong bulls, was secured for the final round
 haripura gujarat main tapti nadi ke kinare ek chota-sa gaanv tha
 Bose Haripura arrived by car to attend this session hosted by Sardar Patel
 gordon iskaa ullekh nahin karte ki yah car ford ve-8 thi yaa nahin
 Elder Henry Ford or his executives knew only in 1938 that even the majestic British Raj could not foresee that power was moving from one base to another and that the era of empire was surrendering to egalitarian nationalism
 ford congress ke mantriyon ke saath rishte banane main nivesh kar rahe the
 By 1938, the Congress had tasted power
 1937 ke chunaavon ke baad congress aadha darjan se zyada british praanton main chunakar ai thi, lekin use lakhanu ke nagar nigam par aadhipaty se dilli main ek swatantra sarkaar banane tak lambii duuri tay kerani thi
 Whoever believed in Haripura in February 1938 that India would be free in nine years, must have been thinking from the heart, not the mind
 vinaashkari vishwa yuddh ne angrejon ke iraade ko post kar diya; or hitler ke khilaaf yah yuddh bhi 18 maah ke baad hua tha
 If Hitler had not become a completely genocidal freak, Britain's powerful appeasement lobby would have kept the country away from this war
 hitler ko isse koi gurej nahin tha ki angrej bharat par shashan karen; usne iskaa samarthan lagbhag utani sargarmi ke saath kiya jitani hasarat se vah britain par germany ke shashan ke sapane dekhtaa tha
 In the long run, no power could prevent India from gaining independence, but if Hitler had not exhausted Britain, the freedom struggle for India could have been a violent and prolonged process
 itihaas kii sabase mahaan vidambnaaon main se ek baat yah he ki 1945 kii haar se germany to ubar gaya, lekin british samrajya jeet ke baad bhi kabhi ubar nahin paaya

 saket sthit jila adaalat ke ek chote se khachaakhach bhare kamare main faisla sunaate hue atirikt satr nyaayadhish yogesh khanna ne chaaron ko samuhik dushkarm, hatya, peedita ke purush mitra kii hatya ke prayaas, aprakritik aparaadh, saboot mitaane, dakaiti or anya araparadhik dhaaraon ke tahat doshi tehraaya
 The court said that all the facts held him responsible for the 'brutal murder' of the 'helpless victim'
 nyaayadhish ne kaha, "chah logon ne ek-ekkar uske saath dushkarm kiya or lohe kii chad va haath uske pet main ghuseda gaya
 His internal organs were taken out of the body
 yah pahalu peedita ko lage ghaav kii gambhirtha ko darshata he
 "he said that the physical wounds inflicted on the victim by the accused, including '18 wounds' to internal organs, were 'dangerous' and sufficient for 'her death
' peedita ke mata-pita or bhai ne bhi isi tarah kii bhaavana vyakt kii
 The victim's mother said, "I want the death penalty for everyone and only then i will get peace
" " The four accused, Mukesh, Pawan Gupta, Vinay Sharma and Akshay Thakur, are in jail since they were arrested
 jis samay adaalat ne apana faisla sunaaya ve sabhi adaalat main maujuud the
 After hearing the court verdict, Vinay Sharma started crying and Mukesh's parents also started crying
 adaalat ne kaha ki peedita ke sharir main doshiyon ne use maar daalane kii 'niyat' se rod ghuseda
 The court said, "after the gang rape, the rod can be inserted and the internal organs pulled out can only be seen as executing the murder
" " In its 237-page judgment, the court stated that the wounds were inflicted in a 'brutal manner' and that the death did not result from an accident
 nyaayadhish khanna ne kaha ki doshiyon ke karname kii prakruti yah sabit karata he ki inamen se koi bhi aavesh main nahin tha balki 'spasht rup se yah tathy sthapit karata he inkaa karnama purvaniyojit tha
 ' jis tareeke se rad kaa istemaal kiya gaya or peedita ke sharir par lage ghaav is sambhaavna ko bal dete hai ki aropiyon ne 'peedita ko kaabo main karne ke liye' rod kaa istemaal kiya
 The victim died 13 days after the brutal attack caused by the wound
 adaalat ne kaha, "peedita kii maut doshiyon dwaara lagaae gaye ghaav ke kaaran hui
 Such a wound has been described by doctors as dangerous, extremely bad for healing and sufficient for death
 "tippaniyan The judge said that the testimony of the complainant (male friend of the victim) present in the bus was 'important' in reaching a conclusion in the case
 is maamle ke chah aropiyon main se ek ne dilli kii tihaad jail main aatmahatya kar lee, jabaki ek kishor aaropee ko 31 disambar ko kishor nyaay board ne teen varsh ke liye sudhaar grih bhej diya
 The board considered that the juvenile accused was involved in the rape and murder
 is ghatana se na keval pradarshnon kaa silsilaa shuru hua, balki baari jan dabaav ke kaaran sansad ne dushkarm ke khilaaf kanoon ko or kathor kiya

 saket sthit jila adaalat ke ek chote se khachaakhach bhare kamare main faisla sunaate hue atirikt satr nyaayadhish yogesh khanna ne chaaron ko samuhik dushkarm, hatya, peedita ke purush mitra kii hatya ke prayaas, aprakritik aparaadh, saboot mitaane, dakaiti or anya araparadhik dhaaraon ke tahat doshi tehraaya

 His internal organs were taken out of the body
 yah pahalu peedita ko lage ghaav kii gambhirtha ko darshata he
 "he said that the physical wounds inflicted on the victim by the accused, including '18 wounds' to internal organs, were 'dangerous' and sufficient for 'her death
' peedita ke mata-pita or bhai ne bhi isi tarah kii bhaavana vyakt kii
 The victim's mother said, "I want the death penalty for everyone and only then i will get peace
" " The four accused, Mukesh, Pawan Gupta, Vinay Sharma and Akshay Thakur, are in jail since they were arrested
 jis samay adaalat ne apana faisla sunaaya ve sabhi adaalat main maujuud the
 After hearing the court verdict, Vinay Sharma started crying and Mukesh's parents also started crying
 adaalat ne kaha ki peedita ke sharir main doshiyon ne use maar daalane kii 'niyat' se rod ghuseda
 The court said, "after the gang rape, the rod can be inserted and the internal organs pulled out can only be seen as executing the murder
" " In its 237-page judgment, the court stated that the wounds were inflicted in a 'brutal manner' and that the death did not result from an accident
 nyaayadhish khanna ne kaha ki doshiyon ke karname kii prakruti yah sabit karata he ki inamen se koi bhi aavesh main nahin tha balki 'spasht rup se yah tathy sthapit karata he inkaa karnama purvaniyojit tha
 ' jis tareeke se rad kaa istemaal kiya gaya or peedita ke sharir par lage ghaav is sambhaavna ko bal dete hai ki aropiyon ne 'peedita ko kaabo main karne ke liye' rod kaa istemaal kiya
 The victim died 13 days after the brutal attack caused by the wound
 adaalat ne kaha, "peedita kii maut doshiyon dwaara lagaae gaye ghaav ke kaaran hui
 Such a wound has been described by doctors as dangerous, extremely bad for healing and sufficient for death
 "tippaniyan The judge said that the testimony of the complainant (male friend of the victim) present in the bus was 'important' in reaching a conclusion in the case
 is maamle ke chah aropiyon main se ek ne dilli kii tihaad jail main aatmahatya kar lee, jabaki ek kishor aaropee ko 31 disambar ko kishor nyaay board ne teen varsh ke liye sudhaar grih bhej diya
 The board considered that the juvenile accused was involved in the rape and murder
 doshi tehraae gaye logon ko buudhvaar ko sajaa sunai jaaegi, lekin inhen maut kii sajaa die jane kii maang nariwadi kaaryakartaaon se lekar vipakshi bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) kii netaa sushamaa swaraj tak ne kii he
 While awarding the verdict in a small packed room of the district court in Saket, Additional Sessions Judge Yogesh Khanna sentenced the four under gang rape, murder, attempt to murder the victim's male friend, unnatural offenses, eradication of evidence, robbery and other criminal offenses
 Convicted
 adaalat ne kaha ki tathyon se sabhi 'asahaay peedita' kii 'nrisansh hatya' ke liye jimmevaar thaharte hai
 The judge said, "six people raped her one by one and an iron rod and hand were punched in her stomach
 uske aantarik ang ko sharir se baahar nikaala gaya
 This aspect shows the severity of the wound to the victim
 " unhone kaha ki aantarik angon ko lage '18 ghaavon' sahit aropiyon dwaara peedita ke lagaae gaye shaareerik ghaav 'khatarnaak' the or 'uski maut' ke liye paryaapt the
 The victim's parents and brother also expressed a similar sentiment
 peedita kii maa ne kaha, "main sabhi ke liye maut kii sajaa chaahati hum or keval tabhi mujhe shanti milegi
 " chaaron aaropee, mukesh, pawan gupta, vinay sharma or akshay thakur giraftaar kiye jane ke baad se jail main band hai
 At the time the court delivered its verdict, they were all present in the court
 adaalat kaa faisla sunne ke baad vinay sharma rone laga or mukesh ke mata-pita bhi rone lage
 The court said that in the victim's body, the accused entered the rod with the 'intention' to kill her
 adaalat ne kaha, "samuhik dushkarm ke baad rod ghusedane or aantarik angon ko baahar khinchne ko hatya ko anjaam dene ke rup main hi dekha ja saktaa he
 " 237 prishthon ke apane faisle main adaalat ne kaha he ki 'krurtapurna tareeke' se ghaav lagaae gaye or maut bhi durghatana se nahin hui he
 Judge Khanna said that the nature of the accused's conviction proves that none of them were in charge but 'clearly establishes the fact that their act was premeditated
 ' The manner in which the raid was used and the wounds on the victim's body add to the possibility that the accused used the rod 'to control the victim'
 ghaav ke kaaran krur hamale ke 13 dinon baad peedita kii maut ho gai
 The court said, "the victim died due to a wound inflicted by the convicts
" aise ghaav ko chikitsakon dwaara khatarnaak, chikitsa ke liye atyant kharaab or maut ke liye paryaapt qaraar diya gaya he
 "comments nyaayadhish ne kaha ki bas main maujuud shikayatakarta (peedita ke purush mitra) kii gavaahi maamle main nishkarsh tak pahunchane main 'mahatvapurn' he
 One of the six accused in the case committed suicide in Delhi's Tihar Jail, while a juvenile accused was sent to the juvenile justice board for three years on December 31 by the juvenile justice board
 board ne mana ki kishor aaropee ko dushkarm or hatya main shaamil tha

According to news agency IANS, researcher Catherine Toney of the Barcelona Institute for Global Health said, "the results of our research suggest that there is a need to further study air pollution in low and middle income countries, because the population and Due to the level of air pollution, there can be a considerable difference in the results of studies of these countries compared to high income countries
